    <p>\n212:     There is a side benefit of this decision. \"inventory-updates\" topic\n * and processes them idempotently.\n */\npublic class InventoryConsumer {\n    private final KafkaConsumer<String, String> consumer;\n    private final Set<String> processedMessages;\n    private volatile boolean running = true;\n\n    /**\n     * Constructs an InventoryConsumer with the given bootstrap servers.\n     *\n     * @param bootstrapServers The Kafka broker addresses\n     */\n    public InventoryConsumer(String bootstrapServers) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n\n        // Use ConsumerConfig constants for all configuration keys\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG, bootstrapServers);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_ID_CONFIG, \"inventory-consumer-group\");\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.CLIENT_ID_CONFIG, \"inventory-consumer-client\");\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.KEY_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.VALUE_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG, \"false\");\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.AUTO_OFFSET_RESET_CONFIG, \"earliest\");\n\n        this.consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        this.processedMessages = new HashSet<>();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Starts consuming messages from the inventory-updates topic.\n     * Processes messages idempotently and commits offsets after each batch.\n     */\n    public void start() {\n        try {\n            consumer.subscribe(Collections.singletonList(\"inventory-updates\"));\n\n            while (running) {\n                // Use poll(Duration) API - not the deprecated poll(long)\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n\n                if (!records.isEmpty()) {\n                    // Process batch of records\n                    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                        processRecord(record);\n                    }\n\n                    // Commit offsets synchronously after processing each batch\n                    consumer.commitSync();\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            // Handle WakeupException for clean shutdown\n            System.err.println(\"Consumer was woken up for shutdown\");\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            System.err.println(\"Error in consumer: \" + e.getMessage());\n            e.printStackTrace();\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n            System.out.println(\"Consumer closed\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Processes a single consumer record idempotently.\n     * Tracks processed messages to ensure exactly-once semantics.\n     *\n     * @param record The consumer record to process\n     */\n    private void processRecord(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        String messageKey = record.key() + \"-\" + record.partition() + \"-\" + record.offset();\n\n        // Idempotent processing: skip if we've already processed this exact message\n        if (processedMessages.contains(messageKey)) {\n            System.out.println(\"Skipping duplicate message: \" + messageKey);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Process the inventory update\n        System.out.println(\"Processing inventory update - Key: \" + record.key() +\n                         \", Value: \" + record.value() +\n                         \", Partition: \" + record.partition() +\n                         \", Offset: \" + record.offset());\n\n        // Mark message as processed for idempotency\n        processedMessages.add(messageKey);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Stops the consumer gracefully.\n     */\n    public void stop() {\n        running = false;\n        consumer.wakeup();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Main method to demonstrate usage\n     */\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        if (args.length < 1) {\n            System.err.println(\"Usage: java InventoryConsumer processedMessages;\n    private volatile boolean running = true;\n\n    /**\n     * Constructs an InventoryConsumer with the given bootstrap servers.\n     *\n     * @param bootstrapServers The Kafka broker addresses\n     */\n    public InventoryConsumer(String bootstrapServers) {\n        Properties props = new Properties();\n\n        // Use ConsumerConfig constants for all configuration keys\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG, bootstrapServers);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.GROUP_ID_CONFIG, \"inventory-consumer-group\");\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.CLIENT_ID_CONFIG, \"inventory-consumer-client\");\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.KEY_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.VALUE_DESERIALIZER_CLASS_CONFIG, StringDeserializer.class);\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG, \"false\");\n        props.put(ConsumerConfig.AUTO_OFFSET_RESET_CONFIG, \"earliest\");\n\n        this.consumer = new KafkaConsumer<>(props);\n        this.processedMessages = new HashSet<>();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Starts consuming messages from the inventory-updates topic.\n     * Processes messages idempotently and commits offsets after each batch.\n     */\n    public void start() {\n        try {\n            consumer.subscribe(Collections.singletonList(\"inventory-updates\"));\n\n            while (running) {\n                // Use poll(Duration) API - not the deprecated poll(long)\n                ConsumerRecords<String, String> records = consumer.poll(Duration.ofSeconds(1));\n\n                if (!records.isEmpty()) {\n                    // Process batch of records\n                    for (ConsumerRecord<String, String> record : records) {\n                        processRecord(record);\n                    }\n\n                    // Commit offsets synchronously after processing each batch\n                    consumer.commitSync();\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (WakeupException e) {\n            // Handle WakeupException for clean shutdown\n            System.err.println(\"Consumer was woken up for shutdown\");\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            System.err.println(\"Error in consumer: \" + e.getMessage());\n            e.printStackTrace();\n        } finally {\n            consumer.close();\n            System.out.println(\"Consumer closed\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Processes a single consumer record idempotently.\n     * Tracks processed messages to ensure exactly-once semantics.\n     *\n     * @param record The consumer record to process\n     */\n    private void processRecord(ConsumerRecord<String, String> record) {\n        String messageKey = record.key() + \"-\" + record.partition() + \"-\" + record.offset();\n\n        // Idempotent processing: skip if we've already processed this exact message\n        if (processedMessages.contains(messageKey)) {\n            System.out.println(\"Skipping duplicate message: \" + messageKey);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Process the inventory update\n        System.out.println(\"Processing inventory update - Key: \" + record.key() +\n                         \", Value: \" + record.value() +\n                         \", Partition: \" + record.partition() +\n                         \", Offset: \" + record.offset());\n\n        // Mark message as processed for idempotency\n        processedMessages.add(messageKey);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Stops the consumer gracefully.\n     */\n    public void stop() {\n        running = false;\n        consumer.wakeup();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Main method to demonstrate usage\n     */\n    public static void main(String[] args) {\n        if (args.length < 1) {\n            System.err.println(\"Usage: java InventoryConsumer <bootstrap-servers>\");\n            System.exit(1);\n        }\n\n        String bootstrapServers = args[0];\n        InventoryConsumer consumer = new InventoryConsumer(bootstrapServers);\n\n        // Add shutdown hook for graceful shutdown\n        Runtime.getRuntime().addShutdownHook(new Thread(() -> {\n            System.out.println(\"Shutting down consumer...\");\n            consumer.stop();\n        }));\n\n        consumer.start();\n    }\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
